                         A cute and charming 1920's Old Spanish-style apartment located just 3 blocks from Cabrillo Beach in San Pedro, CA Our 1- Bedroom includes a large living room area, full kitchen, dining area, full bathroom, DirecTV and a washer &amp; dryer.

                        <div data-reactid="442">
                         Located in historic San Pedro - LA County's own harbor beach town. There are tons of fun activities and things to do in this little gem of a town! A 5-minute drive to: -Ports O'Call for some delicious seafood, live entertainment and fun -Crafted Marketplace: a year-round craft marketplace featuring handmade goods and crafts -San Pedro Harbor which offers waterfront dining, whale watching, and excursions to Catalina Island -The USS Iowa battleship -LA Maritime Museum A 20-minute drive to: -Long Beach Aquarium -Queen Mary -Long Beach Airport A 35-minute drive to: -LAX Airport Our apartment is nestled in the Point Fermin area of the town which is a quiet and relaxing neighborhood just 3 blocks away from Cabrillo Beach. -A 5-minute walk in either direction to: A lovely beach market with food and goodies -A 5-minute walk to: Two of San Pedro's finest cafes - a must if you're craving a delicious meal, especially breakfast or brunch -A 10-minute walk to: The Korean Friendship Bell and Marine Mammal Center -A 15-minute walk to: Historic Point Fermin Park and Lighthouse - take your camera for spectacular ocean and Catalina views
                        </div>

                        <div data-reactid="576">
                         The Easy Breezy Portside Guesthouse is in historic downtown San Pedro. Walk to Ports O' Call, USS Iowa, the Los Angeles waterfront, and the downtown restaurants and art galleries. Enjoy our cute 1920s cottage, which is perfect for relaxing and with easy access to Southern California attractions in Los Angeles, Long Beach and Orange County. It's a perfect getaway for couples, solo adventurers, and business travelers.

                        <div data-reactid="577">
                         Enjoy our open and airy one bedroom cottage. It's nice mixture of old historic touches with brand new renovations. Restored double-hung windows allow for lots of natural light and coastal breezes. Spacious kitchen stocked with all of your cooking and dining essentials. Coffee and tea available. The living room includes a queen-size murphy bed for traveling companions that don't want to share a bed. Brand new queen-size mattress and bedding in the bedroom. Custom bathroom renovation with glass tiled walk-in shower and spacious vanity. Closet with laundry access. Lovely front porch for relaxing. The house has wireless internet and TV access with Netflix, Showtime and Sling TV (streaming television with some network and cable channels). Living room and bedroom have ceiling fans.

                        <div data-reactid="578">
                         We are located in the Vinegar Hill historic district of San Pedro, which is a quaint and quiet area with people from all walks of life. It gets it's name from the wine that locals used to make in the basements of homes in the area! We even have our very own wine making shop and authentic Italian market one block away. Walk two blocks north to the downtown district of 6th and 7th streets, which has a "Main Street" feel to it with lovely architecture and local businesses. Enjoy the restaurants, art galleries, bars and shops that fill downtown, which hosts an Art Walk the first Thursday of the month. Walk two block east to explore the harbor, Ports O' Call Village, and the Maritime Museum. We are a short drive or bike ride (2-3 miles) to Cabrillo Beach, Point Fermin Lighthouse, and other sights on the southern tip of the peninsula. Or just walk our lovely neighborhood and town and take in the spirit of this historic port town!

                        <div data-reactid="742">
                         Attention Please: For whom has big/tall body size friend this boat may only fit in two or three because there are two double bed normally count for two person sleeping together on each and two singal bed for each person. The boat actually designed for six person crew with six bed spot when go fishing over sea as a fishing boat with tigh space inside so if you or any of your friend have big body size then please consider the space or prepare for sharing bed situation. This is an old boat from the 80s nothing really wrong about it but just old like if u open windows and close again the ruber parts may leak some water when it is raining because the ruber is old and may get in middle of the window track. So please make sure close the windows fully after you opened it. The front double bed window has already been sealed cannot be open. Things like this about this boat so please understand this is not a fancy yacht but a place to chill on water and sleep over with low cost for a different experience and be gentle with it please, thank you so much!

                        <div data-reactid="744">
                         <li data-reactid="745"><p data-reactid="746">We stayed for 3 days and it was a really good experience. Xun is a very good host. Friendly and on time in meeting us. He even bought new kitchen supplies just for our stay. The place is clean and met our expectations. Overall we were very pleased with our choice. Thanks Xun! :-D From Lisa &amp; Daniel</p><span data-reactid="747">Daniel</span><span data-reactid="748">2017-02-19T00:00:00Z</span></li>
                         <li data-reactid="749"><p data-reactid="750">Overall, staying on the boat was a good adventure and for those who are hearty sound sleepers looking for something different than a box motel along a busy street, this could be the place. There is a kayak available on the boat, and we used that and brought our own stand-up paddleboards and enjoyed cruising around the harbor in the mornings before the wind piped up. It was fun being right on the harbor - though potential guests beware, the Long Beach Harbor is kind of a weird mix of heavy industry and pleasure boats and you begin to wonder if you've entered some type of Matrix time warp looking out at the cranes and huge container ships nearby. 4 of us staying on the boat was too many, though there are beds for even more. Note that the double bed is pretty small for 2 people (common on boats), so it's best to plan on no more than 3 people, one on each bed. And, boats are no place for light sleepers so if you count yourself as one, don't plan on sleeping well here. Check in with the host about bedding. Everyone, bring ear plugs - regular fridge, clock, water lapping, boats passing, train whistles from the port, and more noises on boats are plentiful. The beauty of lights reflecting on water can make up for those inconveniences. Parking was easy when we got there late Friday night. Our host met us - kind of necessary since instructions are needed about the boat, and access in and out of the locked dock area is difficult. Do make sure to ask for an extra key to the dock gate. As is duly noted, there is a small toilet on board, and regular bathrooms on land - normal for boat slips. You have to be flexible and comfortable with sharing facilities. Host Xun was helpful and ready to please and all in all, we had a good adventure. </p><span data-reactid="751">Aimee</span><span data-reactid="752">2017-03-26T00:00:00Z</span></li>

                         Authentic Mid Century decor with colorful modern flair. Our 1969 home has retro art &amp; furnishings. Easy 110/405 freeway access to all parts of Los Angeles &amp; Orange County. Relax in our master bedroom w/private bath &amp; balcony with cool ocean breezes.

                        <div data-reactid="953">
                         Welcome to the best hidden Mid-Century Modern gem in Los Angeles! We nicknamed our home "The Dream Chasers' Retreat" for the guests we meet who visit and move to Los Angeles pursuing a dream. This city is full of amazing, creative visitors and locals who dream big. We are offering a modern, calming master bedroom with an amazing 260 degree view around the South Bay from the private balcony. The bright private en-suite bathroom has a lovely walk in shower. The bed is a comfortable queen size bed. This room is the master bedroom in The Dream Chaser's Retreat.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="954">
                         Our lovely home is in Harbor City, the southern most part of Los Angeles. This is 1 block east of Torrance and 2 miles from Redondo Beach. It is a safe, tranquil and quiet neighborhood. Most residents enjoy walking their dogs and getting outside to exercise daily. This neighborhood was built in 1969, when Mid-Century Modern met 1970s Retro designs. Within a 15-20 minute drive is Redondo Beach, Torrance Beach, San Pedro and Downtown Long Beach. Popular local destinations nearby are: - Redondo Beach Pier seafood bars &amp; restaurants, plus stunning sunsets - Torrance Beach bike path - Palos Verdes' cliff hiking to tide pools - Long Beach's Convention Center - San Pedro Cruise Warf &amp; Ports-O-Call - Old Town Torrance charm When eating out, our home is convenient to many different types of food: - Korean markets, BBQ &amp; Tofu House - Hawaiian restaurants - Japanese markets, bakeries, Ramen &amp; Sushi - Traditional American breakfast cafes - Asian Fusion restaurants (eg: Peruvian-Japanese, Chinese-Peruvian, Korean-Chinese) Across the street, Mulligans Family Fun is a great place for mini-golf/arcades. It's a one-of-a-kind experience staying at our colorful home.

                        <div data-reactid="1330">
                         Completely remodeled, sunny, open, home in the East Village, with a spacious back yard. Centrally located only a .5 mile from the beach, metro and downtown. Dog friendly, walking distance to tons of great restaurants. It is a shared bathroom. Please read detail description.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1331">
                         We've recently remodeled our entire home, the greenest ways possible, as we both work from home, it's important to us to have a healthy space. Being on the second floor, there is lots of light. Both units have dogs who love guests. So feel free to bring yours as well if they are friendly too. Pets will incur an additional $10/night on top of the airbnb fee. Last minute bookers, unfortunately I do not take same day bookings as I have not had good experiences in the past. Please provide at least 48 hours notice out of courtesy. Production: we have been used at a production site for TV/commercials in the past. Production shoots start at $400/day. Please inquire via message!
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1332">
                         We do live on a busy street, so traffic starts up around 7am. It's generally very quiet though. We have also recently remodeled our backyard. It is now complete with a full kitchen, seating area, storage, SAUNA, outdoor shower, fire pit and garden that we absolutely encourage you to enjoy!

                         The Turret Room is in the Turret House located in the historic Willmore District of downtown Long Beach. Built in 1906, this Victorian is on the historical building register. The room is private with private bath across the hall. It is a small cozy room best for solo travelers. The property includes a lovely courtyard with outside seating for guests to enjoy. The house is within walking distance of the Convention Center, beaches and lots of downtown action. Public transport is available nearby.
